   <h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" lang="en">List of countries by incarceration rate</h1> 
   <div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content"> 
    <div id="siteSub" class="noprint">
     From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia
    </div> 
    <div id="contentSub"></div> 
    <div id="contentSub2"></div> 
    <div id="jump-to-nav"></div> <a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">Jump to navigation</a> <a class="mw-jump-link" href="#searchInput">Jump to search</a>

     <div class="mw-parser-output">

      </div> 
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:502px;">
        <a href="/wiki/File:Prisoners_world_map_png2.png" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Prisoners_world_map_png2.png/500px-Prisoners_world_map_png2.png" decoding="async" width="500" height="273" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Prisoners_world_map_png2.png/750px-Prisoners_world_map_png2.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Prisoners_world_map_png2.png/1000px-Prisoners_world_map_png2.png 2x" data-file-width="2640" data-file-height="1440"></a> 
        <div class="thumbcaption">

          <a href="/wiki/File:Prisoners_world_map_png2.png" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a>

        </div>

      <div style="clear:both;"></div> 
      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Incarceration_totals_and_rates">Incarceration totals and rates</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_countries_by_incarceration_rate&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Incarceration totals and rates">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <p>The table source does not list an incarceration rate for the <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">United Kingdom</a> as a whole. In the list see <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom:_England_%26_Wales" class="mw-redirect" title="United Kingdom: England &amp; Wales">United Kingdom: England &amp; Wales</a>, <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom:_Northern_Ireland" class="mw-redirect" title="United Kingdom: Northern Ireland">United Kingdom: Northern Ireland</a>, <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom:_Scotland" class="mw-redirect" title="United Kingdom: Scotland">United Kingdom: Scotland</a>. A rate for the United Kingdom as a whole can be calculated by adding up the prison populations, and then dividing by the combined population of the UK. </p>
      <p>For info on North Korea, see <a href="#North_Korea">notes below</a>. The <a href="/wiki/World_Prison_Brief" title="World Prison Brief">World Prison Brief</a> (WPB) may or may not incorporate <a href="/wiki/Juvenile_incarceration" class="mw-redirect" title="Juvenile incarceration">juvenile incarceration</a> numbers into the totals for each country. See the individual WPB country pages for more information.<sup id="cite_ref-WorldPrisonBrief_1-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WorldPrisonBrief-1">[1]</a></sup> </p> 
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <b>"Notes" column</b> links to <a href="#Notes">notes section</a> below the chart.
       </dd> 
       <dd>
        <b>"c." (<a href="/wiki/Circa" title="Circa">circa</a>)</b> indicates "approximately". <a href="/wiki/Help:Sorting" title="Help:Sorting">Sorting</a> will not work correctly if it is in front of the number. So it has been removed from <a href="/wiki/Egypt" title="Egypt">Egypt</a>, <a href="/wiki/Honduras" title="Honduras">Honduras</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mauritania" title="Mauritania">Mauritania</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Namibia" title="Namibia">Namibia</a> prison population numbers.
       </dd> 
       <dd>
        <b>Year:</b> The data in the table below is the latest available for each country or territory at the time the data was copied from the World Prison Brief.<sup id="cite_ref-WorldPrisonBrief_1-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WorldPrisonBrief-1">[1]</a></sup>
       </dd>
      </dl>

       </caption>

      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Notes">Notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_countries_by_incarceration_rate&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Notes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <p><i><a href="#Main_table">Return to top of main table.</a></i> </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Europe">Europe</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_countries_by_incarceration_rate&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Europe">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <p>Prison population of <a href="/wiki/Europe" title="Europe">Europe</a> is approximately 1.2 million<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2">[2]</a></sup> of total 743 million population.<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">[3]</a></sup> </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Australia">Australia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_countries_by_incarceration_rate&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Australia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
       Further information: <a href="/wiki/Immigration_detention_in_Australia" title="Immigration detention in Australia">Immigration detention in Australia</a> and <a href="/wiki/Punishment_in_Australia" title="Punishment in Australia">Punishment in Australia</a>
      </div> 
      <p>With a prison population of 42,000 and a total 2018 population of 25 million, <a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australia</a> has an incarceration rate of 171 per 100,000 population, or 222 per 100,000 <b>adult</b> population.<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">[4]</a></sup> </p>
      <p>In addition to its standard prisons, Australia also operates a separate system of <a href="/wiki/Australian_immigration_detention_facilities" title="Australian immigration detention facilities">immigration prisons</a> to detain foreigners who have breached the terms of, or lack a <a href="/wiki/Travel_visa" title="Travel visa">visa</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">[5]</a></sup> Some of these immigration detention centres are used to <a href="/wiki/Indefinite_detention_without_trial" class="mw-redirect" title="Indefinite detention without trial">indefinitely</a> detain<sup id="cite_ref-auto_6-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto-6">[6]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Asylum_in_Australia" title="Asylum in Australia">asylum seekers</a> and <a href="/wiki/Refugees" class="mw-redirect" title="Refugees">refugees</a>, including children,<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">[7]</a></sup> often without <a href="/wiki/Criminal_trial" class="mw-redirect" title="Criminal trial">trial</a>, sometimes for several years.<sup id="cite_ref-auto_6-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto-6">[6]</a></sup> Immigration detainees are not included in the data for prison population and incarceration rates.<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">[8]</a></sup> </p>
      <p>Additionally, the number of prisoners and incarceration rate differs for each Australian <a href="/wiki/States_and_territories_of_Australia" title="States and territories of Australia">state and territory</a>, with some having much higher or lower incarceration rates than the national average. </p>
      <p>In addition to adult prisoners, on an average night in June 2017, there was 964 <a href="/wiki/Minor_(law)" title="Minor (law)">minors</a> imprisoned in Australia.<sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">[9]</a></sup> </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="China">China</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_countries_by_incarceration_rate&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: China">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
       Further information: <a href="/wiki/Re-education_through_labor" title="Re-education through labor">Re-education through labor</a>, <a href="/wiki/Laogai" title="Laogai">Laogai</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Xinjiang_re-education_camps" title="Xinjiang re-education camps">Xinjiang re-education camps</a>
      </div> 
      <p>According to the <a href="/wiki/World_Prison_Brief" title="World Prison Brief">World Prison Brief</a>, <a href="/wiki/China" title="China">China</a> had an incarceration rate of 118 per 100,000 as of mid-2015 (for 1,649,804 sentenced prisoners in <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Justice_of_the_People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="Ministry of Justice of the People's Republic of China">Ministry of Justice</a> prisons only). The <a href="/wiki/World_Prison_Brief" title="World Prison Brief">World Prison Brief</a> states that in addition to the sentenced prisoners, there may be more than 650,000 held in detention centers. "A total prison population of 2,300,000 would raise the incarceration rate to 164 per 100,000."<sup id="cite_ref-China_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-China-10">[10]</a></sup> </p>
      <p>After 2015 there was a great increase in the number of people in the <a href="/wiki/Xinjiang_re-education_camps" title="Xinjiang re-education camps">Xinjiang re-education camps</a>. In May 2018, <a href="/wiki/Randall_Schriver" title="Randall Schriver">Randall Schriver</a> of the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Department_of_Defense" title="United States Department of Defense">United States Department of Defense</a> claimed that "at least a million but likely closer to three million citizens" were imprisoned in detention centers in a strong condemnation of the "concentration camps".<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">[11]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-cc2_12-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-cc2-12">[12]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">[13]</a></sup> In August 2018, a <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> human rights panel said that it had received many credible reports that 1 million ethnic <a href="/wiki/Uyghurs" title="Uyghurs">Uyghurs</a> in China have been held in "re-education camps".<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">[14]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">[15]</a></sup> </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Cuba">Cuba</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_countries_by_incarceration_rate&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Cuba">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <p>In January 2020, a former high ranking judge in Cuba leaked secret Cuban government documents that showed the country had the highest incarceration rate in the world at over 90,000 prisoners, with thousands in prison on dubious charges. Documents reviewed by the <a href="/wiki/New_York_Times" class="mw-redirect" title="New York Times">New York Times</a> showed 92% of individuals tried in the country are found guilty. Nearly 4,000 every year are accused of being "antisocial" or "dangerous", which are terms used by the government to charge those that have committed no crime but are viewed by the regime as a risk to the status quo. Those charges have a 99.5% conviction rate. These individuals face summary trials with no right to a defense or to present evidence, according to the former judge. The documents show individuals being sentenced for several years in prison under the category of "anti-social", which can include actions like not belonging to state associated civic organizations or being unemployed. The crime "description" is often identical, appearing to be copy and pasted by police.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">[16]</a></sup> The high incarceration rate in the secret documents is consistent with dissident group claims that the Cuban government's 2012 one-time release of inmate population numbers, when they reported 57,000 inmates, was false. <sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">[17]</a></sup> </p>
      <p>According to <a href="/wiki/Human_Rights_Watch" title="Human Rights Watch">Human Rights Watch</a>, the Cuban government employs arbitrary detention to harass and intimidate regime critics, independent activists, political opponents, and others. Human Rights Watch's 2018 report noted "Cubans who criticize the government face the threat of criminal prosecution. They do not benefit from <a href="/wiki/Due_process" title="Due process">due process</a> guarantees, such as the right to fair and public hearings by a competent and impartial tribunal. In some cases, detainees are released after receiving official warnings, which prosecutors can later use in subsequent criminal trials to show a pattern of delinquent behavior."<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">[18]</a></sup> </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="India">India</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_countries_by_incarceration_rate&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: India">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <p>The prison population of <a href="/wiki/India" title="India">India</a> was 433,003 as of December 31, 2016, according to the <a href="/wiki/World_Prison_Brief" title="World Prison Brief">World Prison Brief</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">[19]</a></sup> According to the National Prison Portal website when viewed on 22 October 2019, the prison population of India is around 473,000.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">[20]</a></sup> </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="North_Korea">North Korea</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_countries_by_incarceration_rate&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: North Korea">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <p>Little information exists regarding <a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korea's</a> incarceration rate. In 2012, the <a href="/wiki/U.S._Committee_for_Human_Rights_in_North_Korea" class="mw-redirect" title="U.S. Committee for Human Rights in North Korea">U.S. Committee for Human Rights in North Korea</a> estimated 150,000 to 200,000 are incarcerated, based on testimonies of defectors from the state police bureau, which roughly equals 600800 people incarcerated per 100,000.<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">[21]</a></sup> For more information, see <a href="/wiki/Prisons_in_North_Korea" title="Prisons in North Korea">Prisons in North Korea</a>. </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="United_Kingdom">United Kingdom</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_countries_by_incarceration_rate&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: United Kingdom">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <p>The main chart source only provides rates for the constituent parts of the <a href="/wiki/UK" class="mw-redirect" title="UK">UK</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-WorldPrisonBrief_1-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WorldPrisonBrief-1">[1]</a></sup> In the above table see <a href="/wiki/Scotland" title="Scotland">Scotland</a>, <a href="/wiki/Northern_Ireland" title="Northern Ireland">Northern Ireland</a>, and <a href="/wiki/England_and_Wales" title="England and Wales">England and Wales</a>. If they are not listed separately, then they can be found listed under the UK listing. </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="United_States">United States</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_countries_by_incarceration_rate&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: United States">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <table border="1" class="wikitable mw-datatable sortable" style="text-align:right; margin-left: 5px; float:right;">

      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
       Further information: <a href="/wiki/United_States_incarceration_rate" title="United States incarceration rate">United States incarceration rate</a> and <a href="/wiki/Comparison_of_United_States_incarceration_rate_with_other_countries" title="Comparison of United States incarceration rate with other countries">Comparison of United States incarceration rate with other countries</a>
      </div> 
      <p>The incarceration rate (per 100,000 population of all ages) is for inmates held in adult facilities in the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a>. It does not include inmates in the custody of correctional facilities operated by departments of corrections in U.S. territories (<a href="/wiki/American_Samoa" title="American Samoa">American Samoa</a>, <a href="/wiki/Guam" title="Guam">Guam</a>, and the <a href="/wiki/U.S._Virgin_Islands" class="mw-redirect" title="U.S. Virgin Islands">U.S. Virgin Islands</a>) and U.S. commonwealths (<a href="/wiki/Northern_Mariana_Islands" title="Northern Mariana Islands">Northern Mariana Islands</a> and <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico" title="Puerto Rico">Puerto Rico</a>).<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">[23]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-cpusa2016_24-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-cpusa2016-24">[24]</a></sup> </p>
      <p>In addition, there were 43,580 juveniles in <a href="/wiki/Juvenile_detention" class="mw-redirect" title="Juvenile detention">juvenile detention</a> in 2017.<sup id="cite_ref-cjrp_22-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-cjrp-22">[22]</a></sup> For more juvenile detention information and numbers, see <a href="/wiki/Youth_incarceration_in_the_United_States" title="Youth incarceration in the United States">Youth incarceration in the United States</a>. </p>
      <p>The incarceration rate in the U.S. varies greatly by <a href="/wiki/U.S._state" title="U.S. state">U.S. state</a>. See: <a href="/wiki/List_of_U.S._states_and_territories_by_incarceration_and_correctional_supervision_rate" title="List of U.S. states and territories by incarceration and correctional supervision rate">List of U.S. states and territories by incarceration and correctional supervision rate</a>. </p>

          <th scope="row" class="navbox-group" style="width:1%">Age of</th>
          <td class="navbox-list navbox-odd hlist" style="text-align:left;border-left-width:2px;border-left-style:solid;width:100%;padding:0px">
           <div style="padding:0em 0.25em">
